    def initialize_encoder(
        lang: str = None,
        model_dir: str = None,
        spm: bool = True,
        laser: str = None,
    ):

    def initialize_encoder(
        lang: str = None,
        model_dir: str = None,
        spm: bool = True,
        laser: str = None,
    ):
        downloader = LaserModelDownloader(model_dir)
        if laser is not None:

                lang = downloader.get_language_code(LASER3_LANGUAGE, lang)
